<review>Hit or miss.
I would only recommend the chow hall to people I am indifferent about because when it's good, it is great! When it's bad though, you better hope your underpaid overworked military dentist can fix those fillings; the rice is routinely 90% perfectly cooked, 10% diamond cutting hard grains. The chicken varies on a steep slope between the most beautiful, succulent chicken you've ever had, to a level I would describe only as cinnamon challenge level dryness. Overall, I eat here by necessity. I find that I am rewarded less often than I am disappointed,  but I stick around for the price and the hope that they will one day aspire to greatness with every meal.< /review><name>Colton Cleveland< /name>< Date>

<Rating>5< /Rating>< Review>
I‚Äôve passed this place for over a decade without ever thinking about stopping in even though I work just a few blocks away. From the outside, it just never really struck me as the kind of place I needed or even wanted to enter, but earlier this week, I got a craving that could only be satisfied by a chili dog or a Hawaiian vacation. Due to lack of funds, I chose the chili dog route.

The building is very unassuming and is empty any time I drive by after 3:30 so I wondered on the walk there if it would be open or even still in business, but lucky me... it was 3:15 and barely still open. I knew what I wanted (CHILI DOG) and noticed a couple variations, including one called a ‚Äúhangover dog‚Äù which basically just adds jalape√±os (the LAST thing I crave when I‚Äôm hungover).

ANYWAY...  the place is old but immaculate, the staff was incredibly friendly, and the chili dog kicked a$$!! As shown in the photo I took, a random ray of sun poked perfectly through the clouds and the window to shine right on the center of it just before my first bite. (Disclaimer: Wonder Burger is not officially endorsed or blessed by your favorite supreme being.)

OK, OK, I‚Äôm getting carried away here, but seriously... I‚Äôm sooo glad I went and will definitely be back. If you‚Äôre in the area and are craving some really awesome food hot off a greasy grill, give them a try.  You might be disappointed, but then again, you might also be a butthead.  Hahaha!  JK ;-)<//Review>

<Rate>5<//Rate>< Text>
I've had my dog for 11 years. As a puppy I took her to Pet Vets but when I moved out of the area I had to find a new vet. I recently moved back into town and after noticing several bumps on my dog and a huge reduction in her energy level and general interest in things, I became very concerned and brought her back to pet vets.

Despite having to stay in the car during her exam due to cova-19, I still had a great experience with this office.

The staff was very caring and took the time to make sure my dog felt comfortable with them before taking her away for the appointment.

There was an extensive amount of testing and examination that needed to be done and I never felt like I was being overcharged or nickel and dimed.

The vet took extra time to let me ask any questions I needed to and made sure that we covered all the bases to ensure my dogs health stayed optimal as she moved into old age.

Incase you were wondering, all the bumps turned out to be benign and the fatigue and apathetic attitude was stemming from arthritis and not something more serious.

Two weeks into her medication and new diet my dog is back to her old self.

I love this vet and highly recommend it!< /Text>

<rating>5< /rating>< text>
I have been coming here for years, beginning with their location next to Wal-Mart.  There have been growing pains and naturally not every experience is perfect, but all in all I love them!  Consider also that it takes a bit of research to find what is wrong with your pet.  This is not an exact science, and if you have a sick animal you are likely already in a very bad humor.  I have tried different vets (simply because they were closer to home) and have paid much more for much less.  Their prices are very reasonable when compared to other veterinary services, and I feel like the complaints about their fees here are unjustified.  I have had to have several animals put down over the years, and I received no less sympathy and comfort when I had to have a pet rat put to sleep than when I have had to have a dog or a cat euthanized.  Lots of different doctors, open on Saturdays, try a few different vets at this location.  I promise you there is one here who will suit you.<//text>

< Review>
Staff works well together to help you.  My daughter and I both have dental and orthodontic work done at Waterford.  We originally looked here because of the proximity to home, but even now that we're across town, we still enjoy the office.  The front office works well to find appointments that work with our schedule, and we have both had great results with our orthodontic work.  The front and back office seems to get along well, which is nice.  I've been to other offices where that is not the case, and it feels very awkward to visit.  The staff at Waterford is always friendly and professional, and they seem to have updated technology when it comes to their record keeping and tools.  That gives me more confidence about the work than some outdated offices I've been to in the past.
Waterford also has a points system that offers rewards.  You get points for elected services and even for showing up on time to your appointments.  When you accumulate points, you can get rewarded with perks and gift cards.<//Review>

<gmapID>0x80951e0c52596a31:0xaade7af4da2c78a6</gmapID><review>TL,DR: Avoid this place if you are a trucker and like to make money.  Staff is okay, place seems severely disorganized.

I normally don't go around leaving negative reviews, but this is one of the most disorganized shipping facilities I've been to. The staff were friendly enough, so it was more of a left hand didn't know what the right hand was doing kind of thing .

I arrived at about 1230 for my 1300 appointment and checked in. Was told I'd have a little wait, so no big deal at first. I also noticed everytime I came in the dock was a cluster of pallets.  Maybe they had some sort of system to it, but I couldn't tell.

I checked back 2 hours later and they seemed to have "misplaced" my load papers with my name/number/info on it .So, after about 5 minutes they were able to finally print out a new sheet and I filled that out.  I was told I still had a 5-6 hour wait. Starting to get rediculous, but I know things get backed up some times .

Fast forward to about 0100 hours (12 hours after having checked in).  The night crew is no on and I check to see what's going on.  Lo and behold, they can't find my paperwork anywhere. So, after 5 more minutes of the guy messing with the computer, we fill out yet another sheet with the same info. This time I'm told there are 7 trucks ahead of me. When I ask how that's so since I've been waiting for so long (and have been watching trucks that arrived way after me get loaded), I'm met with the response of "I wasn't here when you checked in."  Good job answering my question.

So the next morning, after sitting for 20+ hours at this point, I'm pulled off the load and sent elsewhere. As a courtesy, I go in to let the office know I'm leaving.  I got to wait another 5 minutes while they tried to (and finally did) find my paperwork .

Everytime I went in, it seemed a vast majority of the paperwork was in random spots throughout the office.  This place seriously needs to rethink what they are doing.  Had I stayed there, I would've maybe had one driving shift (11 hours max) to drive over 1,000 miles for the delivery.<//review><pics>None</pics><username>Robby Wideman<//username><time>1556170331449< /time><rate>1<//rate>< UserId.>

< Rating>
4</Rating>
< review>
Finally, another tasty milk tea shop that doesn't require waiting in horrendous lines, or driving all the way down to South Bay!

After lunch at Usagi the other day, my friend and I dropped in to try their creama teas, with myself getting the black tea cream. Being somewhat lactose intolerant, I wasn't about to mix in the entire layer of floated salted cream/milk on top, which ended up being for the better: less is more (flavor), here. My friend, having mixed the entire layer in, found it to be a little too rich and salty, while my drink, with only about a 1/4 or 1/3 swirled in, was light and tasty, still allowing the natural tea flavors to shine through.

At 20 minutes away, with a lot of other great food options nearby, Sharetea will probably become my new go-to milk tea spot.

***Accessibility Info***

Venue - Plenty of space inside the venue, so maneuvering isn't much of an issue, but bear in mind that most, if not all, the seating consisted of smaller two person tables.

Bathroom - Didn't try, so no comment.< /review>

ShareTea is definitely one of my new favorite bubble tea/boba shops around town now!Their teas are consistently great (love that their tapioca balls are soft and chewy) and they don't skimp on the boba!

The prices are slightly higher (~$4 +up) but you can taste the difference in the quality of their drinks. They have a pretty extensive menu and you must at least try out their crema drinks once.

< Review>
Mmm boba. Having worked in a boba shop during high school, I know my boba and can tell the difference. Sharetea had a massive line out the door so we knew it was going to be good. Line took about 20 minutes and then another 5 minutes wait for the drink. Got a okinawa pearl milk tea, which is brown sugar milk tea. It was a little twist on the traditional milk tea and was super yummy. I always get the milk tea when I go to a new boba place...you can really tell the quality of the place by this. The boba was also excellent, perfectly cooked. They mix small and big boba, which I don't really like but that's just my preference. Definitely one of the better boba places in the bay, better than most in SF for sure.< /Review>

<Review>My go-to curry place. The green curry is a must have.

Whenever I get the urge for some curry, I always go here. I've tried out a couple of other places in neighboring cities, but none seem to match Narai Thai. The green curry with chicken is my fav; Something about the texture of the bamboo shoots completes the meal and makes it unmatchable to me.

Family and friends enjoy the red and yellow curry, as well as the pad thai. I recommend trying the salmon steak. And if you have room for dessert, you can't go wrong with the seasonal mango sticky rice.
